00177     #define YY_LESS_LINENO(n)

00179 /* Return all but the first "n" matched characters back to the input stream. */
00180 #define yyless(n) \
00181         do \
00182                 { \
00183                 /* Undo effects of setting up yytext. */ \
00184         int yyless_macro_arg = (n); \
00185         YY_LESS_LINENO(yyless_macro_arg);\
00186                 *yy_cp = yyg->yy_hold_char; \
00187                 YY_RESTORE_YY_MORE_OFFSET \
00188                 yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yy_cp = yy_bp + yyless_macro_arg - YY_MORE_ADJ; \
00189                 YY_DO_BEFORE_ACTION; /* set up yytext again */ \
00190                 } \
00191         while ( 0 )

00202 struct yy_buffer_state
00203         {
00204         FILE *yy_input_file;
00205 
00206         char *yy_ch_buf;                /* input buffer */
00207         char *yy_buf_pos;               /* current position in input buffer */
00208 
00209         /* Size of input buffer in bytes, not including room for EOB
00210          * characters.
00211          */
00212         yy_size_t yy_buf_size;
00213 
00214         /* Number of characters read into yy_ch_buf, not including EOB
00215          * characters.
00216          */
00217         int yy_n_chars;
00218 
00219         /* Whether we "own" the buffer - i.e., we know we created it,
00220          * and can realloc() it to grow it, and should free() it to
00221          * delete it.
00222          */
00223         int yy_is_our_buffer;
00224 
00225         /* Whether this is an "interactive" input source; if so, and
00226          * if we're using stdio for input, then we want to use getc()
00227          * instead of fread(), to make sure we stop fetching input after
00228          * each newline.
00229          */
00230         int yy_is_interactive;
00231 
00232         /* Whether we're considered to be at the beginning of a line.
00233          * If so, '^' rules will be active on the next match, otherwise
00234          * not.
00235          */
00236         int yy_at_bol;
00237 
00238     int yy_bs_lineno; /**< The line count. */
00239     int yy_bs_column; /**< The column count. */
00240     
00241         /* Whether to try to fill the input buffer when we reach the
00242          * end of it.
00243          */
00244         int yy_fill_buffer;
00245 
00246         int yy_buffer_status;
00247 
00248 #define YY_BUFFER_NEW 0
00249 #define YY_BUFFER_NORMAL 1
00250         /* When an EOF's been seen but there's still some text to process
00251          * then we mark the buffer as YY_EOF_PENDING, to indicate that we
00252          * shouldn't try reading from the input source any more.  We might
00253          * still have a bunch of tokens to match, though, because of
00254          * possible backing-up.
00255          *
00256          * When we actually see the EOF, we change the status to "new"
00257          * (via mimosa_http_request_restart()), so that the user can continue scanning by
00258          * just pointing yyin at a new input file.
00259          */
00260 #define YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING 2
00261 
00262         };

00265 /* We provide macros for accessing buffer states in case in the
00266  * future we want to put the buffer states in a more general
00267  * "scanner state".
00268  *
00269  * Returns the top of the stack, or NULL.
00270  */

00272                           ? yyg->yy_buffer_stack[yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top] \

00276  * NULL or when we need an lvalue. For internal use only.
00277  */
00278 #define YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE yyg->yy_buffer_stack[yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top]

00342 /* Done after the current pattern has been matched and before the
00343  * corresponding action - sets up yytext.

00345 #define YY_DO_BEFORE_ACTION \
00346         yyg->yytext_ptr = yy_bp; \
00347         yyleng = (size_t) (yy_cp - yy_bp); \
00348         yyg->yy_hold_char = *yy_cp; \
00349         *yy_cp = '\0'; \
00350         yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yy_cp;

05332 /* Copy whatever the last rule matched to the standard output. */
05333 #ifndef ECHO
05334 /* This used to be an fputs(), but since the string might contain NUL's,
05335  * we now use fwrite().
05336  */
05337 #define ECHO do { if (fwrite( yytext, yyleng, 1, yyout )) {} } while (0)
05338 #endif

05340 /* Gets input and stuffs it into "buf".  number of characters read, or YY_NULL,
05341  * is returned in "result".
05342  */
05343 #ifndef YY_INPUT
05344 #define YY_INPUT(buf,result,max_size) \
05345         errno=0; \
05346         while ( (result = read( fileno(yyin), (char *) buf, max_size )) < 0 ) \
05347         { \
05348                 if( errno != EINTR) \
05349                 { \
05350                         YY_FATAL_ERROR( "input in flex scanner failed" ); \
05351                         break; \
05352                 } \
05353                 errno=0; \
05354                 clearerr(yyin); \
05355         }\
05356 \
05357 
05358 #endif
05359 
05360 /* No semi-colon after return; correct usage is to write "yyterminate();" -
05361  * we don't want an extra ';' after the "return" because that will cause
05362  * some compilers to complain about unreachable statements.
05363  */
05364 #ifndef yyterminate
05365 #define yyterminate() return YY_NULL
05366 #endif

05764                          * possible that this happened because the user
05765                          * just pointed yyin at a new source and called
05766                          * mimosa_http_request_lex().  If so, then we have to assure
05767                          * consistency between YY_CURRENT_BUFFER and our
05768                          * globals.  Here is the right place to do so, because
05769                          * this is the first action (other than possibly a
05770                          * back-up) that will match for the new input source.

05773                         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_input_file = yyin;
05774                         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status = YY_BUFFER_NORMAL;
05775                         }

05777                 /* Note that here we test for yy_c_buf_p "<=" to the position
05778                  * of the first EOB in the buffer, since yy_c_buf_p will
05779                  * already have been incremented past the NUL character
05780                  * (since all states make transitions on EOB to the
05781                  * end-of-buffer state).  Contrast this with the test
05782                  * in input().
05783                  */
05784                 if ( yyg->yy_c_buf_p <= &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[yyg->yy_n_chars] )
05785                         { /* This was really a NUL. */
05786                         yy_state_type yy_next_state;
05787 
05788                         yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yyg->yytext_ptr + yy_amount_of_matched_text;
05789 
05790                         yy_current_state = yy_get_previous_state( yyscanner );
05791 
05792                         /* Okay, we're now positioned to make the NUL
05793                          * transition.  We couldn't have
05794                          * yy_get_previous_state() go ahead and do it
05795                          * for us because it doesn't know how to deal
05796                          * with the possibility of jamming (and we don't
05797                          * want to build jamming into it because then it
05798                          * will run more slowly).
05799                          */
05800 
05801                         yy_next_state = yy_try_NUL_trans( yy_current_state , yyscanner);
05802 
05803                         yy_bp = yyg->yytext_ptr + YY_MORE_ADJ;
05804 
05805                         if ( yy_next_state )
05806                                 {
05807                                 /* Consume the NUL. */
05808                                 yy_cp = ++yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
05809                                 yy_current_state = yy_next_state;
05810                                 goto yy_match;
05811                                 }
05812 
05813                         else
05814                                 {
05815                                 yy_cp = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
05816                                 goto yy_find_action;
05817                                 }
05818                         }
05819 
05820                 else switch ( yy_get_next_buffer( yyscanner ) )
05821                         {
05822                         case EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE:
05823                                 {
05824                                 yyg->yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof = 0;
05825 
05826                                 if ( mimosa_http_request_wrap(yyscanner ) )
05827                                         {
05828                                         /* Note: because we've taken care in
05829                                          * yy_get_next_buffer() to have set up
05830                                          * yytext, we can now set up
05831                                          * yy_c_buf_p so that if some total
05832                                          * hoser (like flex itself) wants to
05833                                          * call the scanner after we return the
05834                                          * YY_NULL, it'll still work - another
05835                                          * YY_NULL will get returned.
05836                                          */
05837                                         yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yyg->yytext_ptr + YY_MORE_ADJ;
05838 
05839                                         yy_act = YY_STATE_EOF(YY_START);
05840                                         goto do_action;
05841                                         }
05842 
05843                                 else
05844                                         {
05845                                         if ( ! yyg->yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof )
05846                                                 YY_NEW_FILE;
05847                                         }
05848                                 break;
05849                                 }
05850 
05851                         case EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN:
05852                                 yyg->yy_c_buf_p =
05853                                         yyg->yytext_ptr + yy_amount_of_matched_text;
05854 
05855                                 yy_current_state = yy_get_previous_state( yyscanner );
05856 
05857                                 yy_cp = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
05858                                 yy_bp = yyg->yytext_ptr + YY_MORE_ADJ;
05859                                 goto yy_match;
05860 
05861                         case EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH:
05862                                 yyg->yy_c_buf_p =
05863                                 &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[yyg->yy_n_chars];
05864 
05865                                 yy_current_state = yy_get_previous_state( yyscanner );
05866 
05867                                 yy_cp = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
05868                                 yy_bp = yyg->yytext_ptr + YY_MORE_ADJ;
05869                                 goto yy_find_action;
05870                         }
05871                 break;
05872                 }
05873 
05874         default:
05875                 YY_FATAL_ERROR(
05876                         "fatal flex scanner internal error--no action found" );
05877         } /* end of action switch */
05878                 } /* end of scanning one token */
05879 } /* end of mimosa_http_request_lex */
05880 
05881 /* yy_get_next_buffer - try to read in a new buffer
05882  *
05883  * Returns a code representing an action:
05884  *      EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH -
05885  *      EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN - continue scanning from current position
05886  *      EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE - end of file
05887  */
05888 static int yy_get_next_buffer (yyscan_t yyscanner)
05889 {
05890     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
05891         register char *dest = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf;
05892         register char *source = yyg->yytext_ptr;
05893         register int number_to_move, i;
05894         int ret_val;
05895 
05896         if ( yyg->yy_c_buf_p > &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[yyg->yy_n_chars + 1] )
05897                 YY_FATAL_ERROR(
05898                 "fatal flex scanner internal error--end of buffer missed" );
05899 
05900         if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_fill_buffer == 0 )
05901                 { /* Don't try to fill the buffer, so this is an EOF. */
05902                 if ( yyg->yy_c_buf_p - yyg->yytext_ptr - YY_MORE_ADJ == 1 )
05903                         {
05904                         /* We matched a single character, the EOB, so
05905                          * treat this as a final EOF.
05906                          */
05907                         return EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE;
05908                         }
05909 
05910                 else
05911                         {
05912                         /* We matched some text prior to the EOB, first
05913                          * process it.
05914                          */
05915                         return EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH;
05916                         }
05917                 }
05918 
05919         /* Try to read more data. */
05920 
05921         /* First move last chars to start of buffer. */
05922         number_to_move = (int) (yyg->yy_c_buf_p - yyg->yytext_ptr) - 1;
05923 
05924         for ( i = 0; i < number_to_move; ++i )
05925                 *(dest++) = *(source++);
05926 
05927         if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status == YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING )
05928                 /* don't do the read, it's not guaranteed to return an EOF,
05929                  * just force an EOF
05930                  */
05931                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = yyg->yy_n_chars = 0;
05932 
05933         else
05934                 {
05935                         int num_to_read =
05936                         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size - number_to_move - 1;
05937 
05938                 while ( num_to_read <= 0 )
05939                         { /* Not enough room in the buffer - grow it. */
05940 
05941                         /* just a shorter name for the current buffer */
05942                         YY_BUFFER_STATE b = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER;
05943 
05944                         int yy_c_buf_p_offset =
05945                                 (int) (yyg->yy_c_buf_p - b->yy_ch_buf);
05946 
05947                         if ( b->yy_is_our_buffer )
05948                                 {
05949                                 int new_size = b->yy_buf_size * 2;
05950 
05951                                 if ( new_size <= 0 )
05952                                         b->yy_buf_size += b->yy_buf_size / 8;
05953                                 else
05954                                         b->yy_buf_size *= 2;
05955 
05956                                 b->yy_ch_buf = (char *)
05957                                         /* Include room in for 2 EOB chars. */
05958                                         mimosa_http_request_realloc((void *) b->yy_ch_buf,b->yy_buf_size + 2 ,yyscanner );
05959                                 }
05960                         else
05961                                 /* Can't grow it, we don't own it. */
05962                                 b->yy_ch_buf = 0;
05963 
05964                         if ( ! b->yy_ch_buf )
05965                                 YY_FATAL_ERROR(
05966                                 "fatal error - scanner input buffer overflow" );
05967 
05968                         yyg->yy_c_buf_p = &b->yy_ch_buf[yy_c_buf_p_offset];
05969 
05970                         num_to_read = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size -
05971                                                 number_to_move - 1;
05972 
05973                         }
05974 
05975                 if ( num_to_read > YY_READ_BUF_SIZE )
05976                         num_to_read = YY_READ_BUF_SIZE;
05977 
05978                 /* Read in more data. */
05979                 YY_INPUT( (&YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[number_to_move]),
05980                         yyg->yy_n_chars, (size_t) num_to_read );
05981 
05982                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = yyg->yy_n_chars;
05983                 }
05984 
05985         if ( yyg->yy_n_chars == 0 )
05986                 {
05987                 if ( number_to_move == YY_MORE_ADJ )
05988                         {
05989                         ret_val = EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE;
05990                         mimosa_http_request_restart(yyin  ,yyscanner);
05991                         }
05992 
05993                 else
05994                         {
05995                         ret_val = EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH;
05996                         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status =
05997                                 YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING;
05998                         }
05999                 }
06000 
06001         else
06002                 ret_val = EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN;
06003 
06004         if ((yy_size_t) (yyg->yy_n_chars + number_to_move) > YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size) {
06005                 /* Extend the array by 50%, plus the number we really need. */
06006                 yy_size_t new_size = yyg->yy_n_chars + number_to_move + (yyg->yy_n_chars >> 1);
06007                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf = (char *) mimosa_http_request_realloc((void *) YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf,new_size ,yyscanner );
06008                 if ( ! YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf )
06009                         YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_get_next_buffer()" );
06010         }
06011 
06012         yyg->yy_n_chars += number_to_move;
06013         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[yyg->yy_n_chars] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
06014         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[yyg->yy_n_chars + 1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
06015 
06016         yyg->yytext_ptr = &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[0];
06017 
06018         return ret_val;
06019 }
06020 
06021 /* yy_get_previous_state - get the state just before the EOB char was reached */
06022 
06023     static yy_state_type yy_get_previous_state (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06024 {
06025         register yy_state_type yy_current_state;
06026         register char *yy_cp;
06027     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06028 
06029         yy_current_state = yy_start_state_list[yyg->yy_start];
06030 
06031         for ( yy_cp = yyg->yytext_ptr + YY_MORE_ADJ; yy_cp < yyg->yy_c_buf_p; ++yy_cp )
06032                 {
06033                 yy_current_state += yy_current_state[(*yy_cp ? YY_SC_TO_UI(*yy_cp) : 256)].yy_nxt;
06034                 if ( yy_current_state[-1].yy_nxt )
06035                         {
06036                         yyg->yy_last_accepting_state = yy_current_state;
06037                         yyg->yy_last_accepting_cpos = yy_cp;
06038                         }
06039                 }
06040 
06041         return yy_current_state;
06042 }
06043 
06044 /* yy_try_NUL_trans - try to make a transition on the NUL character
06045  *
06046  * synopsis
06047  *      next_state = yy_try_NUL_trans( current_state );
06048  */
06049     static yy_state_type yy_try_NUL_trans  (yy_state_type yy_current_state , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06050 {
06051         register int yy_is_jam;
06052     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner; /* This var may be unused depending upon options. */
06053         register char *yy_cp = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06054 
06055         register int yy_c = 256;
06056         register yyconst struct yy_trans_info *yy_trans_info;
06057 
06058         yy_trans_info = &yy_current_state[(unsigned int) yy_c];
06059         yy_current_state += yy_trans_info->yy_nxt;
06060         yy_is_jam = (yy_trans_info->yy_verify != yy_c);
06061 
06062         if ( ! yy_is_jam )
06063                 {
06064                 if ( yy_current_state[-1].yy_nxt )
06065                         {
06066                         yyg->yy_last_accepting_state = yy_current_state;
06067                         yyg->yy_last_accepting_cpos = yy_cp;
06068                         }
06069                 }
06070 
06071         return yy_is_jam ? 0 : yy_current_state;
06072 }
06073 
06074     static void yyunput (int c, register char * yy_bp , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06075 {
06076         register char *yy_cp;
06077     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06078 
06079     yy_cp = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06080 
06081         /* undo effects of setting up yytext */
06082         *yy_cp = yyg->yy_hold_char;
06083 
06084         if ( yy_cp < YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf + 2 )
06085                 { /* need to shift things up to make room */
06086                 /* +2 for EOB chars. */
06087                 register int number_to_move = yyg->yy_n_chars + 2;
06088                 register char *dest = &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[
06089                                         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size + 2];
06090                 register char *source =
06091                                 &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[number_to_move];
06092 
06093                 while ( source > YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf )
06094                         *--dest = *--source;
06095 
06096                 yy_cp += (int) (dest - source);
06097                 yy_bp += (int) (dest - source);
06098                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars =
06099                         yyg->yy_n_chars = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size;
06100 
06101                 if ( yy_cp < YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf + 2 )
06102                         YY_FATAL_ERROR( "flex scanner push-back overflow" );
06103                 }
06104 
06105         *--yy_cp = (char) c;
06106 
06107         yyg->yytext_ptr = yy_bp;
06108         yyg->yy_hold_char = *yy_cp;
06109         yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yy_cp;
06110 }
06111 
06112 #ifndef YY_NO_INPUT
06113 #ifdef __cplusplus
06114     static int yyinput (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06115 #else
06116     static int input  (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06117 #endif
06118 
06119 {
06120         int c;
06121     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06122 
06123         *yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yyg->yy_hold_char;
06124 
06125         if ( *yyg->yy_c_buf_p == YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR )
06126                 {
06127                 /* yy_c_buf_p now points to the character we want to return.
06128                  * If this occurs *before* the EOB characters, then it's a
06129                  * valid NUL; if not, then we've hit the end of the buffer.
06130                  */
06131                 if ( yyg->yy_c_buf_p < &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[yyg->yy_n_chars] )
06132                         /* This was really a NUL. */
06133                         *yyg->yy_c_buf_p = '\0';
06134 
06135                 else
06136                         { /* need more input */
06137                         int offset = yyg->yy_c_buf_p - yyg->yytext_ptr;
06138                         ++yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06139 
06140                         switch ( yy_get_next_buffer( yyscanner ) )
06141                                 {
06142                                 case EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH:
06143                                         /* This happens because yy_g_n_b()
06144                                          * sees that we've accumulated a
06145                                          * token and flags that we need to
06146                                          * try matching the token before
06147                                          * proceeding.  But for input(),
06148                                          * there's no matching to consider.
06149                                          * So convert the EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH
06150                                          * to EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE.
06151                                          */
06152 
06153                                         /* Reset buffer status. */
06154                                         mimosa_http_request_restart(yyin ,yyscanner);
06155 
06156                                         /*FALLTHROUGH*/
06157 
06158                                 case EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE:
06159                                         {
06160                                         if ( mimosa_http_request_wrap(yyscanner ) )
06161                                                 return EOF;
06162 
06163                                         if ( ! yyg->yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof )
06164                                                 YY_NEW_FILE;
06165 #ifdef __cplusplus
06166                                         return yyinput(yyscanner);
06167 #else
06168                                         return input(yyscanner);
06169 #endif
06170                                         }
06171 
06172                                 case EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN:
06173                                         yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yyg->yytext_ptr + offset;
06174                                         break;
06175                                 }
06176                         }
06177                 }
06178 
06179         c = *(unsigned char *) yyg->yy_c_buf_p; /* cast for 8-bit char's */
06180         *yyg->yy_c_buf_p = '\0';        /* preserve yytext */
06181         yyg->yy_hold_char = *++yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06182 
06183         return c;
06184 }
06185 #endif  /* ifndef YY_NO_INPUT */
06186 
06187 /** Immediately switch to a different input stream.
06188  * @param input_file A readable stream.
06189  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06190  * @note This function does not reset the start condition to @c INITIAL .
06191  */
06192     void mimosa_http_request_restart  (FILE * input_file , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06193 {
06194     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06195 
06196         if ( ! YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ){
06197         mimosa_http_request_ensure_buffer_stack (yyscanner);
06198                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE =
06199             mimosa_http_request__create_buffer(yyin,YY_BUF_SIZE ,yyscanner);
06200         }
06201 
06202         mimosa_http_request__init_buffer(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER,input_file ,yyscanner);
06203         mimosa_http_request__load_buffer_state(yyscanner );
06204 }
06205 
06206 /** Switch to a different input buffer.
06207  * @param new_buffer The new input buffer.
06208  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06209  */
06210     void mimosa_http_request__switch_to_buffer  (YY_BUFFER_STATE  new_buffer , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06211 {
06212     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06213 
06214         /* TODO. We should be able to replace this entire function body
06215          * with
06216          *              mimosa_http_request_pop_buffer_state();
06217          *              mimosa_http_request_push_buffer_state(new_buffer);
06218      */
06219         mimosa_http_request_ensure_buffer_stack (yyscanner);
06220         if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER == new_buffer )
06221                 return;
06222 
06223         if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
06224                 {
06225                 /* Flush out information for old buffer. */
06226                 *yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yyg->yy_hold_char;
06227                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06228                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = yyg->yy_n_chars;
06229                 }
06230 
06231         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = new_buffer;
06232         mimosa_http_request__load_buffer_state(yyscanner );
06233 
06234         /* We don't actually know whether we did this switch during
06235          * EOF (mimosa_http_request_wrap()) processing, but the only time this flag
06236          * is looked at is after mimosa_http_request_wrap() is called, so it's safe
06237          * to go ahead and always set it.
06238          */
06239         yyg->yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof = 1;
06240 }
06241 
06242 static void mimosa_http_request__load_buffer_state  (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06243 {
06244     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06245         yyg->yy_n_chars = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars;
06246         yyg->yytext_ptr = yyg->yy_c_buf_p = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos;
06247         yyin = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_input_file;
06248         yyg->yy_hold_char = *yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06249 }
06250 
06251 /** Allocate and initialize an input buffer state.
06252  * @param file A readable stream.
06253  * @param size The character buffer size in bytes. When in doubt, use @c YY_BUF_SIZE.
06254  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06255  * @return the allocated buffer state.
06256  */
06257     YY_BUFFER_STATE mimosa_http_request__create_buffer  (FILE * file, int  size , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06258 {
06259         YY_BUFFER_STATE b;
06260     
06261         b = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) mimosa_http_request_alloc(sizeof( struct yy_buffer_state ) ,yyscanner );
06262         if ( ! b )
06263                 YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in mimosa_http_request__create_buffer()" );
06264 
06265         b->yy_buf_size = size;
06266 
06267         /* yy_ch_buf has to be 2 characters longer than the size given because
06268          * we need to put in 2 end-of-buffer characters.
06269          */
06270         b->yy_ch_buf = (char *) mimosa_http_request_alloc(b->yy_buf_size + 2 ,yyscanner );
06271         if ( ! b->yy_ch_buf )
06272                 YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in mimosa_http_request__create_buffer()" );
06273 
06274         b->yy_is_our_buffer = 1;
06275 
06276         mimosa_http_request__init_buffer(b,file ,yyscanner);
06277 
06278         return b;
06279 }
06280 
06281 /** Destroy the buffer.
06282  * @param b a buffer created with mimosa_http_request__create_buffer()
06283  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06284  */
06285     void mimosa_http_request__delete_buffer (YY_BUFFER_STATE  b , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06286 {
06287     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06288 
06289         if ( ! b )
06290                 return;
06291 
06292         if ( b == YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ) /* Not sure if we should pop here. */
06293                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) 0;
06294 
06295         if ( b->yy_is_our_buffer )
06296                 mimosa_http_request_free((void *) b->yy_ch_buf ,yyscanner );
06297 
06298         mimosa_http_request_free((void *) b ,yyscanner );
06299 }
06300 
06301 #ifndef __cplusplus
06302 extern int isatty (int );
06303 #endif /* __cplusplus */
06304     
06305 /* Initializes or reinitializes a buffer.
06306  * This function is sometimes called more than once on the same buffer,
06307  * such as during a mimosa_http_request_restart() or at EOF.
06308  */
06309     static void mimosa_http_request__init_buffer  (YY_BUFFER_STATE  b, FILE * file , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06310 
06311 {
06312         int oerrno = errno;
06313     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06314 
06315         mimosa_http_request__flush_buffer(b ,yyscanner);
06316 
06317         b->yy_input_file = file;
06318         b->yy_fill_buffer = 1;
06319 
06320     /* If b is the current buffer, then mimosa_http_request__init_buffer was _probably_
06321      * called from mimosa_http_request_restart() or through yy_get_next_buffer.
06322      * In that case, we don't want to reset the lineno or column.
06323      */
06324     if (b != YY_CURRENT_BUFFER){
06325         b->yy_bs_lineno = 1;
06326         b->yy_bs_column = 0;
06327     }
06328 
06329         b->yy_is_interactive = file ? (isatty( fileno(file) ) > 0) : 0;
06330     
06331         errno = oerrno;
06332 }
06333 
06334 /** Discard all buffered characters. On the next scan, YY_INPUT will be called.
06335  * @param b the buffer state to be flushed, usually @c YY_CURRENT_BUFFER.
06336  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06337  */
06338     void mimosa_http_request__flush_buffer (YY_BUFFER_STATE  b , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06339 {
06340     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06341         if ( ! b )
06342                 return;
06343 
06344         b->yy_n_chars = 0;
06345 
06346         /* We always need two end-of-buffer characters.  The first causes
06347          * a transition to the end-of-buffer state.  The second causes
06348          * a jam in that state.
06349          */
06350         b->yy_ch_buf[0] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
06351         b->yy_ch_buf[1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
06352 
06353         b->yy_buf_pos = &b->yy_ch_buf[0];
06354 
06355         b->yy_at_bol = 1;
06356         b->yy_buffer_status = YY_BUFFER_NEW;
06357 
06358         if ( b == YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
06359                 mimosa_http_request__load_buffer_state(yyscanner );
06360 }
06361 
06362 /** Pushes the new state onto the stack. The new state becomes
06363  *  the current state. This function will allocate the stack
06364  *  if necessary.
06365  *  @param new_buffer The new state.
06366  *  @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06367  */
06368 void mimosa_http_request_push_buffer_state (YY_BUFFER_STATE new_buffer , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06369 {
06370     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06371         if (new_buffer == NULL)
06372                 return;
06373 
06374         mimosa_http_request_ensure_buffer_stack(yyscanner);
06375 
06376         /* This block is copied from mimosa_http_request__switch_to_buffer. */
06377         if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
06378                 {
06379                 /* Flush out information for old buffer. */
06380                 *yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yyg->yy_hold_char;
06381                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos = yyg->yy_c_buf_p;
06382                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = yyg->yy_n_chars;
06383                 }
06384 
06385         /* Only push if top exists. Otherwise, replace top. */
06386         if (YY_CURRENT_BUFFER)
06387                 yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top++;
06388         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = new_buffer;
06389 
06390         /* copied from mimosa_http_request__switch_to_buffer. */
06391         mimosa_http_request__load_buffer_state(yyscanner );
06392         yyg->yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof = 1;
06393 }
06394 
06395 /** Removes and deletes the top of the stack, if present.
06396  *  The next element becomes the new top.
06397  *  @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06398  */
06399 void mimosa_http_request_pop_buffer_state (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06400 {
06401     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06402         if (!YY_CURRENT_BUFFER)
06403                 return;
06404 
06405         mimosa_http_request__delete_buffer(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ,yyscanner);
06406         YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = NULL;
06407         if (yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top > 0)
06408                 --yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top;
06409 
06410         if (YY_CURRENT_BUFFER) {
06411                 mimosa_http_request__load_buffer_state(yyscanner );
06412                 yyg->yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof = 1;
06413         }
06414 }
06415 
06416 /* Allocates the stack if it does not exist.
06417  *  Guarantees space for at least one push.
06418  */
06419 static void mimosa_http_request_ensure_buffer_stack (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06420 {
06421         int num_to_alloc;
06422     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06423 
06424         if (!yyg->yy_buffer_stack) {
06425 
06426                 /* First allocation is just for 2 elements, since we don't know if this
06427                  * scanner will even need a stack. We use 2 instead of 1 to avoid an
06428                  * immediate realloc on the next call.
06429          */
06430                 num_to_alloc = 1;
06431                 yyg->yy_buffer_stack = (struct yy_buffer_state**)mimosa_http_request_alloc
06432                                                                 (num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*)
06433                                                                 , yyscanner);
06434                 if ( ! yyg->yy_buffer_stack )
06435                         YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in mimosa_http_request_ensure_buffer_stack()" );
06436                                                                   
06437                 memset(yyg->yy_buffer_stack, 0, num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*));
06438                                 
06439                 yyg->yy_buffer_stack_max = num_to_alloc;
06440                 yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top = 0;
06441                 return;
06442         }
06443 
06444         if (yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top >= (yyg->yy_buffer_stack_max) - 1){
06445 
06446                 /* Increase the buffer to prepare for a possible push. */
06447                 int grow_size = 8 /* arbitrary grow size */;
06448 
06449                 num_to_alloc = yyg->yy_buffer_stack_max + grow_size;
06450                 yyg->yy_buffer_stack = (struct yy_buffer_state**)mimosa_http_request_realloc
06451                                                                 (yyg->yy_buffer_stack,
06452                                                                 num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*)
06453                                                                 , yyscanner);
06454                 if ( ! yyg->yy_buffer_stack )
06455                         YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in mimosa_http_request_ensure_buffer_stack()" );
06456 
06457                 /* zero only the new slots.*/
06458                 memset(yyg->yy_buffer_stack + yyg->yy_buffer_stack_max, 0, grow_size * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*));
06459                 yyg->yy_buffer_stack_max = num_to_alloc;
06460         }
06461 }
06462 
06463 /** Setup the input buffer state to scan directly from a user-specified character buffer.
06464  * @param base the character buffer
06465  * @param size the size in bytes of the character buffer
06466  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06467  * @return the newly allocated buffer state object. 
06468  */
06469 YY_BUFFER_STATE mimosa_http_request__scan_buffer  (char * base, yy_size_t  size , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06470 {
06471         YY_BUFFER_STATE b;
06472     
06473         if ( size < 2 ||
06474              base[size-2] != YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR ||
06475              base[size-1] != YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR )
06476                 /* They forgot to leave room for the EOB's. */
06477                 return 0;
06478 
06479         b = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) mimosa_http_request_alloc(sizeof( struct yy_buffer_state ) ,yyscanner );
06480         if ( ! b )
06481                 YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in mimosa_http_request__scan_buffer()" );
06482 
06483         b->yy_buf_size = size - 2;      /* "- 2" to take care of EOB's */
06484         b->yy_buf_pos = b->yy_ch_buf = base;
06485         b->yy_is_our_buffer = 0;
06486         b->yy_input_file = 0;
06487         b->yy_n_chars = b->yy_buf_size;
06488         b->yy_is_interactive = 0;
06489         b->yy_at_bol = 1;
06490         b->yy_fill_buffer = 0;
06491         b->yy_buffer_status = YY_BUFFER_NEW;
06492 
06493         mimosa_http_request__switch_to_buffer(b ,yyscanner );
06494 
06495         return b;
06496 }
06497 
06498 /** Setup the input buffer state to scan a string. The next call to mimosa_http_request_lex() will
06499  * scan from a @e copy of @a str.
06500  * @param yystr a NUL-terminated string to scan
06501  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06502  * @return the newly allocated buffer state object.
06503  * @note If you want to scan bytes that may contain NUL values, then use
06504  *       mimosa_http_request__scan_bytes() instead.
06505  */
06506 YY_BUFFER_STATE mimosa_http_request__scan_string (yyconst char * yystr , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06507 {
06508     
06509         return mimosa_http_request__scan_bytes(yystr,strlen(yystr) ,yyscanner);
06510 }
06511 
06512 /** Setup the input buffer state to scan the given bytes. The next call to mimosa_http_request_lex() will
06513  * scan from a @e copy of @a bytes.
06514  * @param bytes the byte buffer to scan
06515  * @param len the number of bytes in the buffer pointed to by @a bytes.
06516  * @param yyscanner The scanner object.
06517  * @return the newly allocated buffer state object.
06518  */
06519 YY_BUFFER_STATE mimosa_http_request__scan_bytes  (yyconst char * yybytes, int  _yybytes_len , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06520 {
06521         YY_BUFFER_STATE b;
06522         char *buf;
06523         yy_size_t n;
06524         int i;
06525     
06526         /* Get memory for full buffer, including space for trailing EOB's. */
06527         n = _yybytes_len + 2;
06528         buf = (char *) mimosa_http_request_alloc(n ,yyscanner );
06529         if ( ! buf )
06530                 YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in mimosa_http_request__scan_bytes()" );
06531 
06532         for ( i = 0; i < _yybytes_len; ++i )
06533                 buf[i] = yybytes[i];
06534 
06535         buf[_yybytes_len] = buf[_yybytes_len+1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
06536 
06537         b = mimosa_http_request__scan_buffer(buf,n ,yyscanner);
06538         if ( ! b )
06539                 YY_FATAL_ERROR( "bad buffer in mimosa_http_request__scan_bytes()" );
06540 
06541         /* It's okay to grow etc. this buffer, and we should throw it
06542          * away when we're done.
06543          */
06544         b->yy_is_our_buffer = 1;
06545 
06546         return b;
06547 }
06548 
06549     static void yy_push_state (int  new_state , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06550 {
06551     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06552         if ( yyg->yy_start_stack_ptr >= yyg->yy_start_stack_depth )
06553                 {
06554                 yy_size_t new_size;
06555 
06556                 yyg->yy_start_stack_depth += YY_START_STACK_INCR;
06557                 new_size = yyg->yy_start_stack_depth * sizeof( int );
06558 
06559                 if ( ! yyg->yy_start_stack )
06560                         yyg->yy_start_stack = (int *) mimosa_http_request_alloc(new_size ,yyscanner );
06561 
06562                 else
06563                         yyg->yy_start_stack = (int *) mimosa_http_request_realloc((void *) yyg->yy_start_stack,new_size ,yyscanner );
06564 
06565                 if ( ! yyg->yy_start_stack )
06566                         YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of memory expanding start-condition stack" );
06567                 }
06568 
06569         yyg->yy_start_stack[yyg->yy_start_stack_ptr++] = YY_START;
06570 
06571         BEGIN(new_state);
06572 }
06573 
06574     static void yy_pop_state  (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06575 {
06576     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06577         if ( --yyg->yy_start_stack_ptr < 0 )
06578                 YY_FATAL_ERROR( "start-condition stack underflow" );
06579 
06580         BEGIN(yyg->yy_start_stack[yyg->yy_start_stack_ptr]);
06581 }
06582 
06583     static int yy_top_state  (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06584 {
06585     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06586         return yyg->yy_start_stack[yyg->yy_start_stack_ptr - 1];
06587 }

06595         (void) fprintf( stderr, "%s\n", msg );
06596         exit( YY_EXIT_FAILURE );
06597 }

06599 /* Redefine yyless() so it works in section 3 code. */
06600 
06601 #undef yyless
06602 #define yyless(n) \
06603         do \
06604                 { \
06605                 /* Undo effects of setting up yytext. */ \
06606         int yyless_macro_arg = (n); \
06607         YY_LESS_LINENO(yyless_macro_arg);\
06608                 yytext[yyleng] = yyg->yy_hold_char; \
06609                 yyg->yy_c_buf_p = yytext + yyless_macro_arg; \
06610                 yyg->yy_hold_char = *yyg->yy_c_buf_p; \
06611                 *yyg->yy_c_buf_p = '\0'; \
06612                 yyleng = yyless_macro_arg; \
06613                 } \
06614         while ( 0 )

06774 /* User-visible API */
06775 
06776 /* mimosa_http_request_lex_init is special because it creates the scanner itself, so it is
06777  * the ONLY reentrant function that doesn't take the scanner as the last argument.
06778  * That's why we explicitly handle the declaration, instead of using our macros.
06779  */
06780 
06781 int mimosa_http_request_lex_init(yyscan_t* ptr_yy_globals)
06782 
06783 {
06784     if (ptr_yy_globals == NULL){
06785         errno = EINVAL;
06786         return 1;
06787     }
06788 
06789     *ptr_yy_globals = (yyscan_t) mimosa_http_request_alloc ( sizeof( struct yyguts_t ), NULL );
06790 
06791     if (*ptr_yy_globals == NULL){
06792         errno = ENOMEM;
06793         return 1;
06794     }
06795 
06796     /* By setting to 0xAA, we expose bugs in yy_init_globals. Leave at 0x00 for releases. */
06797     memset(*ptr_yy_globals,0x00,sizeof(struct yyguts_t));
06798 
06799     return yy_init_globals ( *ptr_yy_globals );
06800 }
06801 
06802 /* mimosa_http_request_lex_init_extra has the same functionality as mimosa_http_request_lex_init, but follows the
06803  * convention of taking the scanner as the last argument. Note however, that
06804  * this is a *pointer* to a scanner, as it will be allocated by this call (and
06805  * is the reason, too, why this function also must handle its own declaration).
06806  * The user defined value in the first argument will be available to mimosa_http_request_alloc in
06807  * the yyextra field.
06808  */
06809 
06810 int mimosa_http_request_lex_init_extra(YY_EXTRA_TYPE yy_user_defined,yyscan_t* ptr_yy_globals )
06811 
06812 {
06813     struct yyguts_t dummy_yyguts;
06814 
06815     mimosa_http_request_set_extra (yy_user_defined, &dummy_yyguts);
06816 
06817     if (ptr_yy_globals == NULL){
06818         errno = EINVAL;
06819         return 1;
06820     }
06821         
06822     *ptr_yy_globals = (yyscan_t) mimosa_http_request_alloc ( sizeof( struct yyguts_t ), &dummy_yyguts );
06823         
06824     if (*ptr_yy_globals == NULL){
06825         errno = ENOMEM;
06826         return 1;
06827     }
06828     
06829     /* By setting to 0xAA, we expose bugs in
06830     yy_init_globals. Leave at 0x00 for releases. */
06831     memset(*ptr_yy_globals,0x00,sizeof(struct yyguts_t));
06832     
06833     mimosa_http_request_set_extra (yy_user_defined, *ptr_yy_globals);
06834     
06835     return yy_init_globals ( *ptr_yy_globals );
06836 }
06837 
06838 static int yy_init_globals (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06839 {
06840     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06841     /* Initialization is the same as for the non-reentrant scanner.
06842      * This function is called from mimosa_http_request_lex_destroy(), so don't allocate here.
06843      */
06844 
06845     yyg->yy_buffer_stack = 0;
06846     yyg->yy_buffer_stack_top = 0;
06847     yyg->yy_buffer_stack_max = 0;
06848     yyg->yy_c_buf_p = (char *) 0;
06849     yyg->yy_init = 0;
06850     yyg->yy_start = 0;
06851 
06852     yyg->yy_start_stack_ptr = 0;
06853     yyg->yy_start_stack_depth = 0;
06854     yyg->yy_start_stack =  NULL;
06855 
06856 /* Defined in main.c */
06857 #ifdef YY_STDINIT
06858     yyin = stdin;
06859     yyout = stdout;
06860 #else
06861     yyin = (FILE *) 0;
06862     yyout = (FILE *) 0;
06863 #endif
06864 
06865     /* For future reference: Set errno on error, since we are called by
06866      * mimosa_http_request_lex_init()
06867      */
06868     return 0;
06869 }
06870 
06871 /* mimosa_http_request_lex_destroy is for both reentrant and non-reentrant scanners. */
06872 int mimosa_http_request_lex_destroy  (yyscan_t yyscanner)
06873 {
06874     struct yyguts_t * yyg = (struct yyguts_t*)yyscanner;
06875 
06876     /* Pop the buffer stack, destroying each element. */
06877         while(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER){
06878                 mimosa_http_request__delete_buffer(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ,yyscanner );
06879                 YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = NULL;
06880                 mimosa_http_request_pop_buffer_state(yyscanner);
06881         }
06882 
06883         /* Destroy the stack itself. */
06884         mimosa_http_request_free(yyg->yy_buffer_stack ,yyscanner);
06885         yyg->yy_buffer_stack = NULL;
06886 
06887     /* Destroy the start condition stack. */
06888         mimosa_http_request_free(yyg->yy_start_stack ,yyscanner );
06889         yyg->yy_start_stack = NULL;
06890 
06891     /* Reset the globals. This is important in a non-reentrant scanner so the next time
06892      * mimosa_http_request_lex() is called, initialization will occur. */
06893     yy_init_globals( yyscanner);
06894 
06895     /* Destroy the main struct (reentrant only). */
06896     mimosa_http_request_free ( yyscanner , yyscanner );
06897     yyscanner = NULL;
06898     return 0;
06899 }

06929 
06930 void *mimosa_http_request_realloc  (void * ptr, yy_size_t  size , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06931 {
06932         /* The cast to (char *) in the following accommodates both
06933          * implementations that use char* generic pointers, and those
06934          * that use void* generic pointers.  It works with the latter
06935          * because both ANSI C and C++ allow castless assignment from
06936          * any pointer type to void*, and deal with argument conversions
06937          * as though doing an assignment.
06938          */
06939         return (void *) realloc( (char *) ptr, size );
06940 }
06941 
06942 void mimosa_http_request_free (void * ptr , yyscan_t yyscanner)
06943 {
06944         free( (char *) ptr );   /* see mimosa_http_request_realloc() for (char *) cast */
06945 }
